msg:2023 finally came with a walk-and-go trip, decided in the morning, departed at noon, arrived in the afternoon, and finally arrived at the Qinhuangdao Yudao Ocean Hot Spring Resort that we have been thinking about. We booked the 8-meter RV in Feisheersenzeyuan The caravan is very big, the environment is very good, clean and tidy, it is just suitable for our family of 4 big and 1 small, and it satisfies the children's desire to live in a car. It is close to the beach, and the beach and the sea are just outside the door. Walking along the beach, the scenery is very beautiful. In the evening, I ate a buffet on the second floor of the hot spring hotel. There are many varieties and the taste is very good. It is open until 20:30. Walking along the seaside, after returning to our 8-meter caravan, I found that the shower head in the bathroom was not working, and there was no toothbrush. I called the front desk, and a boy answered with a very good attitude. The service staff took a few minutes A toothbrush was delivered, and I asked him to show me the shower. He also adjusted it up and down, but still no water came out, and asked the maintenance personnel to come and take a look. Since we came back, it was already ten o'clock, and there were two more. The old man who is almost 80 years old is too tired, so he didn't let the maintenance personnel come over. I called the front desk and wanted to change us to 2 rooms in the park the next day. We will pay the difference normally, and I will fall asleep tonight. After getting off, the front desk staff said that they need to see if there is any room tomorrow, and they will call me back later. The call back was very fast, and they said they could change us to another RV. But I consider that the bathtub in the bathroom is a bit high, and it is inconvenient for the elderly to go in and take a bath. I still want to change the room in the park the next day. The young boy at the front desk is very kind. He said that he needs to ask the leader for instructions, and he also needs to see if there is any tomorrow. Room. Since we came during the peak tourist season of summer vacation, the 3 hotels in the park are basically out of rooms. Only some high-priced townhouses and suites are left. The price per night is very high, which is not something our ordinary families can afford. We are at a loss. At that time, a boy with a voice like a TV announcer called and said that it was Liu Wenxin, the duty manager of Yudao Senzeyuan. After listening to the front desk about our situation, he asked if it was convenient for us now, and he could take us to see a joint office. The parent-child room in the townhouse is just right for us to live in. There is no need to make up the price difference. We are very happy. In a few minutes, Mr. Liu came to pick us up and showed us the room. On the way, Due to the dark road, Mr. Liu was stuck all over by the big spider web blocking the road, which did not affect his warm service. We were very satisfied with the room we saw. We wanted to move here that night. When we went back to pack our things, he helped us get a new check-in bracelet and room key in advance, and rode an electric car to guide us. Since we were traveling with the elderly and children and had a lot of luggage, Mr. Liu also helped us carry our luggage. When we got down, it was already early in the morning. Mr. Liu left after he settled us down. The old man said that he could finally take a shower. After everyone took a shower, they could finally sleep comfortably. The next day, I soaked in indoor and outdoor hot springs in the resort, watched a Hollywood show, and went grass-skiing. In short, there were too many things to do, and it was impossible to enjoy them all. The fishing island is very suitable for traveling with the elderly and children. It not only accompanies the elderly but also the children. I sincerely thank Mr. Liu Wenxin for his warm and thoughtful service, which allowed us to spend 2 days happily on the fishing island. I sincerely recommend that we go on vacation on the fishing island. Friends, the hardware and software facilities of the fishing island are really good. Thank you again to Mr. Liu Wenxin for making our trip to the fishing island unforgettable. I hope to have the opportunity to visit other facilities that we have not experienced.
